########################################################################
# Events for the Han dynasty
########################################################################

# Wang Mang overthrow the throne
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_HAN.1
	title = "eh_china_HAN.1.t"
	desc = "eh_china_HAN.1.d"
	picture = IMPERIAL_SEAL_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			HND = {
				every_owned_province = {
					add_core = XIN
					remove_core = HND
					remove_core = WEI
					remove_core = WUU
					remove_core = SHU
				}
			}
			XIN = {
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = celestial_empire
				set_government_rank = 3
				set_emperor_of_china = XIN
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_HAN.1.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		XIN = {
			add_army_tradition = -10
			add_army_professionalism = -0.1
			add_adm_tech = 1
			add_dip_tech = 1
			add_mil_tech = 1
			add_treasury = 1000
			inherit = HND
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Mang"
				dynasty = "Wang"
				change_adm = 1
				change_dip = 0
				change_mil = 1
			}
			define_consort = {
				name = "Xiaomu"
				dynasty = "Wang"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				female = yes
			}
			remove_heir = { allow_new_heir = no }
		}
		XIO = {
			add_adm_tech = 1
			add_dip_tech = 1
			add_mil_tech = 2 
		}
	}
}

# Red Eyebrows Rebellion
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_HAN.2
	title = "eh_china_HAN.2.t"
	desc = "eh_china_HAN.2.d"
	picture = ANGRY_MOB_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			HND = {
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = celestial_empire
				set_government_rank = 3
				set_emperor_of_china = HND
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_HAN.2.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		XIN = {
			set_country_flag = lulin_campaign
			change_government = monarchy
			add_government_reform = chinese_warlord
			set_government_rank = 3
			add_stability = -1
			add_prestige = -10
			add_mandate = -10
			add_manpower = -10
			688 = {
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = anti_tax_rebels
					size = 10
					leader = "Fan Chong"
				}
			}
			690 = {
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = anti_tax_rebels
					size = 10
				}
			}
			2141 = {
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = anti_tax_rebels
					size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		HND = {
			set_country_flag = lulin_campaign
			add_treasury = 10000
			add_years_of_income = 1
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Xiu"
				dynasty = "Liu"
				change_adm = 6
				change_dip = 5
				change_mil = 6
				age = 30
				min_age = 30
				max_age = 35
			}
			define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 4	shock = 3	manuever = 1	siege = 2	}
			define_consort = {
				name= "Shengtong"
				dynasty = "Guo"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				female = yes
			}
			define_heir = {
				name = "Zhuang"
				dynasty = "Liu"
				change_adm = 5
				change_dip = 4
				change_mil = 5
				age = 1
			}
			country_event = { id = eh_china_HAN.3 days = 300 }
		}
		LNX = {
			set_country_flag = lulin_campaign
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Ying"
				dynasty = "Liu"
			}
		}
		CEG = {
			set_country_flag = lulin_campaign
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Shu"
				dynasty = "Gongsun"
			}
		}
		HYO = {
			set_country_flag = lulin_campaign
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Shao"
				dynasty = "Wei"
			}
		}
	}
}

# Liu Xiu restored Han dynasty
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_HAN.3
	title = "eh_china_HAN.3.t"
	desc = "eh_china_HAN.3.d"
	picture = IMPERIAL_SEAL_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			HND = {
				inherit = XIN
				inherit = JI0
				inherit = HLI
				inherit = LNX
				inherit = LI2
				inherit = HQN
				inherit = HYA
				inherit = HYI
				inherit = HJZ
				inherit = XU0
				inherit = YOU
			}
			XIN = { clr_country_flag = lulin_campaign }
			LNX = { clr_country_flag = lulin_campaign }
			CEG = { clr_country_flag = lulin_campaign }
			HYO = { clr_country_flag = lulin_campaign }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "eh_china_HAN.3.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		HND = {
			clr_country_flag = lulin_campaign
			add_adm_power = 100
			add_dip_power = 100
			add_mil_power = 100
            add_stability = 3
			add_manpower = 30
			add_sailors = 1000
			add_mandate = 10
			add_army_tradition = 10
			add_army_professionalism = 0.1
			add_meritocracy_effect = yes
            add_prestige = 30
			add_treasury = 10000
			add_years_of_income = 3
			add_war_exhaustion = -10
			set_capital = 1836
			every_owned_province = {
				add_unrest = -0.1
				add_core = HND
				remove_core = XIN
				kill_units = {
					who = REB
					type = infantry
				}
				kill_units = {
					who = REB
					type = cavalry
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Unification of China by the Han dynasty
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_HAN.4
	title = "eh_china_HAN.4.t"
	desc = "eh_china_HAN.4.d"
	picture = IMPERIAL_SEAL_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = HND
		is_year = 35
		NOT = { is_year = 40 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}

	option = {
		name = "eh_china_HAN.4.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		HND = {
			set_country_flag = yellow_turban_rebellion_happened
			inherit = CEG
			inherit = HYO
		}
	}
}

# Protectorate of the Western Regions
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_HAN.5
	title = "eh_china_HAN.5.t"
	desc = "eh_china_HAN.5.d"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = HND
		is_year = 50
		NOT = { is_year = 60 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 700
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			HOT = {
				change_religion = mahayana
				710 = {
					add_base_tax = 1
					add_base_production = 1
					add_base_manpower = 1
					add_prosperity = 1
					cede_province = HOT
					add_core = HOT
					remove_core = KAS
				}
			}
			SHS = { change_religion = mahayana }
			SUE = { change_religion = mahayana }
			KAS = { change_religion = mahayana }
			KUC = { change_religion = mahayana }
			XIY = { change_religion = mahayana }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_HAN.5.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		HND = {
			define_general = {
				name = "Ban Chao"
				shock = 3
				fire = 3
				manuever = 4
				siege = 0
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = tributary_state
				subject = HOT
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = tributary_state
				subject = SHS
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = tributary_state
				subject = SUE
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = tributary_state
				subject = KAS
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = tributary_state
				subject = KUC
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = tributary_state
				subject = XIY
			}
			118 = { discover_country = HND }
			151 = { discover_country = HND }
			410 = { discover_country = HND }
		}
		ROM = {
			700 = { discover_country = ROM }
			707 = { discover_country = ROM }
			1836 = { discover_country = ROM }
		}
		PRT = {
			700 = { discover_country = PRT }
			707 = { discover_country = PRT }
			1836 = { discover_country = PRT }
		}
	}
}

# Yellow Turban
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_HAN.6
	title = "eh_china_HAN.6.t"
	desc = "eh_china_HAN.6.d"
	picture = ANGRY_MOB_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = HND
		is_year = 184
		NOT = { is_year = 187 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_HAN.6.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		HND = {
			set_country_flag = uprising_eh
			add_stability = -1
			add_prestige = -10
			add_mandate = -10
			add_manpower = -10
			add_corruption = 10
			china_superregion = {
				add_unrest = 0.1
				add_devastation = 10
			}
			2140 = {
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = heretic_rebels
					size = 10
					leader = "Zhang Jue"
				}
			}
			692 = {
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = heretic_rebels
					size = 10
					leader = "Zhang Bao"
				}
			}
			4195 = {
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = heretic_rebels
					size = 10
					leader = "Zhang Liang"
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# End of the Han dynasty
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_HAN.7
	title = "eh_china_HAN.7.t"
	desc = "eh_china_HAN.7.d"
	picture = OVEREXTENSION_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = HND
		is_year = 190
		NOT = { is_year = 192 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			HND = {
				add_stability = -1
				add_corruption = 10
				add_prestige = -10
				add_mandate = -10
				add_manpower = -10
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = warlordism
					duration = 2000
				}
				define_ruler = {
					name = "Xie"
					dynasty = "Liu"
					change_adm = 0
					change_dip = 1
					change_mil = 0
					min_age = 9
					max_age = 11
				}
				remove_heir = { allow_new_heir = no }
				china_superregion = {
					limit = { owned_by = HND }
					kill_units = {
						who = REB
						type = infantry
					}
					kill_units = {
						who = REB
						type = cavalry
					}
				}
				1836 = {
					if = {
						limit = { owned_by = HND }
					}
					add_base_tax = -10
					add_base_production = -10
					add_base_manpower = -10
				}
				country_event = { id = eh_china_HAN.8 days = 700 }
			}
			WEI = {
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = chinese_warlord
				set_government_rank = 1
				688 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = WEI }
						}
					}
					cede_province = WEI
					add_core = WEI
					remove_core = HND
				}
				2140 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = WEI }
						}
					}
					cede_province = WEI
					add_core = WEI
					remove_core = HND
				}
				2176 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = WEI }
						}
					}
					cede_province = WEI
					add_core = WEI
					remove_core = HND
				}
				define_ruler = {
					name = "Cao"
					dynasty = "Cao"
					change_adm = 5
					change_dip = 4
					change_mil = 6
					age = 35
				}
				define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 4	shock = 4	manuever = 2	siege = 2 }
				define_consort = {
					name = "Wuxuan"
					dynasty = "Bian"
					change_adm = 2
					change_dip = 2
					change_mil = 2
					female = yes
				}
				define_heir = {
					name = "Pi"
					dynasty = "Cao"
					change_adm = 2
					change_dip = 2
					change_mil = 4
					age = 3
				}
			}
			WUU = {
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = chinese_warlord
				set_government_rank = 1
				south_jiangsu_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = WUU }
							NOT = { province_id = 1822 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = WUU
					add_core = WUU
					remove_core = HND
				}
				define_ruler = {
					name = "Jian"
					dynasty = "Sun"
					change_adm = 2
					change_dip = 1
					change_mil = 5
					age = 35
					claim = 95
				}
				define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 3	shock = 3	manuever = 1	siege = 1 }
				define_consort = {
					dynasty = "Wu"
					change_adm = 2
					change_dip = 2
					change_mil = 2
					female = yes
				}
				define_heir = {
					name = "Ce"
					dynasty = "Sun"
					change_adm = 1
					change_dip = 3
					change_mil = 5
					age = 15
					claim = 95
				}
				define_heir_to_general = {	fire = 3	shock = 3	manuever = 2	siege = 2 }
			}
			ZHO = {
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = chinese_warlord
				set_government_rank = 1
				686 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = ZHO }
						}
					}
					cede_province = ZHO
					add_core = ZHO
					remove_core = HND
				}
				1838 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = ZHO }
						}
					}
					cede_province = ZHO
					add_core = ZHO
					remove_core = HND
				}
				2144 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = ZHO }
						}
					}
					cede_province = ZHO
					add_core = ZHO
					remove_core = HND
				}
				2171 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = ZHO }
						}
					}
					cede_province = ZHO
					add_core = ZHO
					remove_core = HND
				}
				2175 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = ZHO }
						}
					}
					cede_province = ZHO

					cede_province = ZHO

				}
				define_ruler = {

					change_mil = 2

					dynasty = "Feng"
					change_adm = 2
					change_dip = 2
					change_mil = 2
					female = yes
				}
			}
			JI0 = {
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = chinese_warlord
				set_government_rank = 1
				south_hebei_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = JI0 }
							NOT = { province_id = 695 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = JI0
					add_core = JI0
					remove_core = HND
				}
				west_shandong_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = JI0 }

				}

						}

					remove_core = HND
				}
				define_ruler = {
					name = "Shao"
					dynasty = "Yuan"

					claim = 95

				define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 2	shock = 1	manuever = 0	siege = 1 }

# End of the Han dynasty (2)
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_HAN.8
	title = "eh_china_HAN.8.t"
	desc = "eh_china_HAN.8.d"
	picture = OVEREXTENSION_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			HND = {
				set_capital = 687
				add_stability = -1
				add_corruption = 10
				add_prestige = -10
				add_mandate = -10
				add_manpower = -10
				687 = { rename_capital = "Xuedu" }
			}
			WEI = {
				set_country_flag = sanguo_china
				add_stability = 1
				1836 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = WEI }
						}
					}
					cede_province = WEI
					add_core = WEI
					remove_core = HND
				}
				2144 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = WEI }
						}
					}
					cede_province = WEI
					add_core = WEI
					remove_core = ZHO
				}
				2175 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = WEI }
						}
					}
					cede_province = WEI
					add_core = WEI
					remove_core = ZHO
				}
				declare_war_with_cb = {
					who = HYO
					casus_belli = cb_chinese_unification
				}
			}
			JNG = {
				2171 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = JNG }
						}
					}
					cede_province = JNG
					add_core = JNG
					remove_core = ZHO
				}
			}
			HYO = { set_country_flag = sanguo_china }
			HYA = {	add_stability = -1 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_HAN.8.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		WEI = { set_capital = 688 }
		JI0 = { set_capital = 2137 }
		JNG = { set_capital = 2171 }
	}
}

# Wang Mang overthrow the throne - Event for tag
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_HAN.9
	title = "eh_china_HAN.9.t"
	desc = "eh_china_HAN.9.d"
	picture = IMPERIAL_SEAL_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = HND
		is_year = 8
		NOT = { is_year = 10 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			HND = { country_event = { id = eh_china_HAN.1 days = 3 } }
			XIN = {
				700 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = XIN }
						}
					}
					cede_province = XIN
					add_core = XIN
					remove_core = HND
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_HAN.9.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				HND = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = XIN
		}
	}
}

# Green forest Rebellion - Event for tag
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_HAN.10
	title = "eh_china_HAN.10.t"
	desc = "eh_china_HAN.10.d"

	fire_only_once = yes

		tag = XIN
		is_year = 23
		NOT = { is_year = 25 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic

	}

# Rise of the Cao Wei

		tag = HND

					who = HND
					value = 50

				}
			}
			JI0 = {
				inherit = HQN
				shandong_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = JI0 }
					}
					cede_province = JI0
					add_core = JI0
					remove_core = HQN
				}
			}
			HLI = {
				2183 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = HLI }
						}
					}
					cede_province = HLI

# Lu Meng's invasion of Jing Province
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_SANGUO.10
	title = "eh_china_SANGUO.10.t"
	desc = "eh_china_SANGUO.10.d"
	picture = IMPERIAL_SEAL_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = SHU
			tag = WUU
		}
		is_year = 219
		NOT = { is_year = 220 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			HND = {
				every_subject_country = {
					limit = { is_subject_of = HND }
					grant_independence = yes
				}
			}
			SHU = {
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = chinese_warlord
				set_government_rank = 2
				set_capital = 679
				add_legitimacy = 20
				add_prestige = 20
				grant_independence = yes
				define_consort = {
					name = "Mu"
					dynasty = "Wu"
					change_adm = 2
					change_dip = 2
					change_mil = 2
					female = yes
				}
				kill_leader = {
					type = "Guan Yu"
				}
				689 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = SHU }
						}
					}
					cede_province = SHU
					add_core = SHU
					remove_core = HYO
				}
				create_subject = {
					subject_type = tributary_state
					subject = CMI
				}
				create_subject = {
					subject_type = tributary_state
					subject = CYI
				}
				create_subject = {
					subject_type = tributary_state
					subject = HYI
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_SANGUO.10.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

			change_government = monarchy

					}

				cede_province = WUU
				add_core = WUU
				remove_core = SHU
			}
			hunan_area = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { owned_by = WUU }
				}
				cede_province = WUU
				add_core = WUU
				remove_core = SHU

			clr_country_flag = eh_override_name
			restore_country_name = yes 
		}
	}

# End of the Three Kingdoms
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_SANGUO.19
	title = "eh_china_SANGUO.19.t"
	desc = "eh_china_SANGUO.19.d"
	picture = REFORM_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		AND = {
			was_player = yes
			OR = {
				tag = SHU
				tag = WUU
			}
		}
		is_year = 255
		NOT = { is_year = 260 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_SANGUO.19.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				WUU = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = WEI
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHU = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = WEI
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_SANGUO.19.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}

			add_prestige = 10

			inherit = WUU

				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { owned_by = A12 }

						NOT = { province_id = 698 }
						NOT = { province_id = 703 }
						NOT = { province_id = 2181 }

				}

		days = 300
	}

			A12 = {
				set_capital = 1821
				add_stability = 1
				add_prestige = 10
				add_mandate = 10

					name = "Rui"
					dynasty = "Sima"

					change_dip = 4
					change_mil = 2

					max_age = 45
				}
				define_consort = {
					name = "Achun"
					dynasty = "Zheng"

					change_dip = 2
					change_mil = 2

				}
				define_heir = {
					name = "Shao"

					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = HND }
					}
					cede_province = HND

					remove_core = A12

# Sixteen Kingdoms
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_JIN.6
	title = "eh_china_JIN.6.t"
	desc = "eh_china_JIN.6.d"
	picture = MONGOL_BANNERS_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = A12
		is_year = 325
		NOT = { is_year = 335 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 700
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			ZAO = {
				inherit = HND
				gansu_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = ZAO }
							NOT = { province_id = 698 }
							NOT = { province_id = 699 }
							NOT = { province_id = 2181 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = ZAO
					add_core = ZAO
					remove_core = HND
				}
				shaanxi_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = ZAO }
							NOT = { province_id = 689 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = ZAO
					add_core = ZAO
					remove_core = HND
				}
				shanxi_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = ZAO }
					}
					cede_province = ZAO
					add_core = ZAO
					remove_core = HND
				}
			}
			DAX = { grant_independence = yes }
			HLI = { grant_independence = yes }
			SXI = { grant_independence = yes }
			YAN = { grant_independence = yes }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_JIN.6.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		ZAO = {
			create_guarantee = CEG
			define_heir = {
				name = "Hu"
				dynasty = "Shi"
				change_adm = 0
				change_dip = 0
				change_mil = 4
				age = 30
				claim = 95
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = pretender_rebels
					size = 1
				}
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = tributary_state
				subject = DAX
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = tributary_state
				subject = HLI
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = tributary_state
				subject = SXI
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = tributary_state
				subject = YAN
			}
		}
		XIB = { country_event = { id = eh_asia_MON.3 days = 300 } }
	}
}

# Hou Jing Rebellion
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_NANBEICHAO.11
	title = "eh_china_NANBEICHAO.11.t"
	desc = "eh_china_NANBEICHAO.11.d"
	picture = BAD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = LNG
		is_year = 550
		NOT = { is_year = 555 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			LNG = {
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = { area = south_jiangsu_area }
					spawn_rebels = {
						type = noble_rebels
						size = 1
					}
				}
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = { area = south_jiangsu_area }
					spawn_rebels = {
						type = noble_rebels
						size = 1
					}
				}
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = { area = anhui_area }
					spawn_rebels = {
						type = pretender_rebels
						size = 10
						leader = "Hou Jing"
					}
				}
			}
			LNX = {
				huguang_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = LNX }
							NOT = { province_id = 4197 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = LNX
					add_core = LNX
					remove_core = LNG
				}
			}
			WEW = {
				xinan_region = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = WEW }
							NOT = { area = guangxi_area }
							NOT = { area = yun_gui_borderland_area }
							NOT = { province_id = 2170 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = WEW
					add_core = WEW
					remove_core = LNX
				}
				shaanxi_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = WEW }
					}
					cede_province = WEW
					add_core = WEW
					remove_core = LNX
				}
			}
			QIC = {
				2136 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = QIC }
						}
					}
					cede_province = QIC
					add_core = QIC
					remove_core = WEE
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_NANBEICHAO.11.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		LNG = { country_event = { id = eh_china_NANBEICHAO.12 days = 700 } }
		WEE = { country_event = { id = eh_china_NANBEICHAO.16 days = 3 } }
	}
}

# Unification of the Northern China by Northern Zhou
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_SUI.1
	title = "eh_china_SUI.1.t"
	desc = "eh_china_SUI.1.d"
	picture = COURT_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CZH
		is_year = 580
		NOT = { is_year = 585 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}

	option = {
		name = "eh_china_SUI.1.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		CZH = {
			add_stability = 1
			add_prestige = 10
			add_manpower = 10
			add_legitimacy = 10
			add_corruption = -10
			add_inflation = -1
			add_treasury = 10000
			inherit = QIC
			country_event = { id = eh_china_SUI.2 days = 300 }

# Unification of China by the Sui dynasty
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_SUI.3
	title = "eh_china_SUI.3.t"
	desc = "eh_china_SUI.3.d"
	picture = REFORM_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
        tag = SUI
        is_year = 589
		NOT = { is_year = 590 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
    }
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			SUI = {
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = celestial_empire
				set_government_rank = 3
				set_emperor_of_china = SUI
				add_harmonized_religion = mahayana
				add_stability = 1
				add_prestige = 10
				add_treasury = 10000
				add_mandate = 10
				add_war_exhaustion = -10
				701 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = SUI }
						}
					}
					cede_province = SUI
					add_core = SUI
					remove_core = GOK
				}
				704 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = SUI }
						}
					}
					cede_province = SUI
					add_core = SUI
					remove_core = QIC
				}
				702 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = SUI }
						}
					}
					cede_province = SUI
					add_core = SUI
					remove_core = GOK
				}
				4223 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = SUI }
						}
					}
					cede_province = SUI
					add_core = SUI
					remove_core = GOK
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_SUI.3.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		SUI = {
			inherit = CEN
			china_superregion = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { owned_by = SUI }
						NOT = { area = taiwan_area }
						NOT = { area = yun_gui_borderland_area }
						NOT = { province_id = 703 }
					}
				}
				cede_province = SUI
				add_core = SUI
				remove_core = CEN
			}
		}
	}
}

# Unification of China by the Tang dynasty
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_TNG.2
	title = "eh_china_TNG.2.t"
	desc = "eh_china_TNG.2.d"
	picture = REFORM_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			TNG = {
				inherit = CHC
				inherit = LNX
				inherit = XIA
				inherit = YAN
				inherit = WUU
				inherit = LSO
				inherit = ZHE
				china_superregion = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = TNG }
							NOT = { area = taiwan_area }
							NOT = { area = yun_gui_borderland_area }
							NOT = { province_id = 703 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = TNG
					add_core = TNG
					remove_core = ZHE
				}
				red_river_delta_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = TNG }
							NOT = { province_id = 2371 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = TNG
					add_core = TNG
					remove_core = DAI
				}
				vietnam_area = {
					limit = {

							NOT = { owned_by = TNG }
							NOT = { province_id = 2373 }

					}

# Huang Chao Rebellion
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_TNG.17
	title = "eh_china_TNG.17.t"
	desc = "eh_china_TNG.17.d"
	picture = ANGRY_MOB_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = TNG
		is_year = 885
		NOT = { is_year = 890 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 100
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			TNG = {
				set_country_flag = huang_chao_rebellion
				add_stability = -1
				add_mandate = -10
				add_manpower = -10
				add_corruption = 10
				add_army_tradition = -10
				add_army_professionalism = -0.1
				set_capital = 679
				china_superregion = {
					limit = { owned_by = TNG }
					add_devastation = 30
					kill_units = {
						who = TNG
						type = infantry
					}
					kill_units = {
						who = TNG
						type = cavalry
					}
				}
			}
			QIC = {
				set_country_flag = huang_chao_rebellion

					change_dip = 0
					change_mil = 5
					claim = 95
					age = 45
				}
				define_consort = {
					dynasty = "Cao"
					change_adm = 2
					change_dip = 2
					change_mil = 2
					female = yes
				}
				2140 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = QIC }
						}

					cede_province = QIC
					add_core = QIC

					han_banner = QIC
					han_banner = QIC
					manchu_banner = QIC
					manchu_banner = QIC
					manchu_banner = QIC
					manchu_banner = QIC
				}
				700 = {
					han_banner = QIC
					han_banner = QIC
					han_banner = QIC
					han_banner = QIC
					han_banner = QIC
					han_banner = QIC

					han_banner = QIC
					manchu_banner = QIC
					manchu_banner = QIC
					manchu_banner = QIC
					manchu_banner = QIC
				}
				1836 = {
					han_banner = QIC

	option = {

					type = pretender_rebels
					size = 1
					leader = "Wang Shenzhi"
				}
			}
			west_shandong_area = {

				}

				who = TNG

		}

# End of the Tang dynasty (3)
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_TNG.20
	title = "eh_china_TNG.20.t"
	desc = "eh_china_TNG.20.d"
	picture = OVEREXTENSION_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = TNG
		is_year = 905
		NOT = { is_year = 910 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			TNG = { 
				remove_country_modifier = warlordism
				every_subject_country = {
					limit = { is_subject_of = TNG }
					grant_independence = yes
				}
			}
			LNG = {
				add_manpower = 10
				add_sailors = 1000
				huguang_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = LNG }
							NOT = { province_id = 682 }
							NOT = { province_id = 4197 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = LNG
					add_core = LNG
					remove_core = TNG
				}
				create_subject = {
					subject_type = tributary_state
					subject = TNG
				}
				country_event = { id = eh_china_WUDAI.1 days = 700 }
			}
			CHC = {
				add_manpower = 10
				set_capital = 2172
				hunan_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = CHC }
					}
					cede_province = CHC
					add_core = CHC
					remove_core = TNG
				}

						limit = {

					}

					add_core = SHU
					remove_core = TNG
				}
				689 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = SHU }
						}
					}
					cede_province = SHU
					add_core = SHU
					remove_core = QI2
				}
			}
			HNX = {
				add_manpower = 10
				add_sailors = 1000
				set_capital = 667
				inherit = HJZ
				inherit = YUE
				guangdong_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = HNX }
					}
					cede_province = HNX
					add_core = HNX
					remove_core = TNG
				}
				west_guangdong_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = HNX }
					}
					cede_province = HNX
					add_core = HNX
					remove_core = TNG
				}
				2162 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = HNX }
						}
					}
					cede_province = HNX

# Tang Mandate - Minor event
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_TNG.21
	title = "eh_china_TNG.21.t"
	desc = "eh_china_TNG.21.d"
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			OR = {
				tag = SUI
				tag = TNG
			}
		}
		OR = {
			SUI = { is_emperor_of_china = yes }
			TNG = { is_emperor_of_china = yes }
		}
		is_year = 590
		NOT = { is_year = 900 }
		NOT = { imperial_mandate = 50 }
		TNG = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = anshi_rebellion }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = huang_chao_rebellion }
			}
		}
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_TNG.21.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		SUI = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = historical_mandate
				duration = 9000
			}
		}
		TNG = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = historical_mandate
				duration = 95000
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = eh_china_WUDAI.1
	title = "eh_china_WUDAI.1.t"
	desc = "eh_china_WUDAI.1.d"

	major = yes

			LNG = {
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = celestial_empire
				set_government_rank = 3
				set_emperor_of_china = LNG
				add_harmonized_religion = mahayana
				698 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = LNG }
						}
					}
					cede_province = LNG
					add_core = LNG
					remove_core = QI2
				}
				2179 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = LNG }
						}
					}
					cede_province = LNG
					add_core = LNG
					remove_core = QI2
				}
				2181 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = LNG }
						}
					}
					cede_province = LNG
					add_core = LNG
					remove_core = QI2
				}
			}
			A12 = { inherit = YAN }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_WUDAI.1.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		LNG = {
			inherit = TNG

				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = LNG }
					}
				}
				rename_capital = "Jingzhao"
				cede_province = LNG
				add_core = LNG
				remove_core = TNG
			}
		}
		A12 = {
			set_government_rank = 2
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Cunxu"
				dynasty = "Li"
				change_adm = 4
				change_dip = 4
				change_mil = 5
				claim = 95
				age = 22
			}
			define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 3	shock = 4	manuever = 1	siege = 1 }
			define_consort = {
				dynasty = "Han"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				female = yes
			}
			define_heir = {
				name = "Siyuan"
				dynasty = "Li"
				change_adm = 4
				change_dip = 3
				change_mil = 1
				claim = 95
				age = 40
			}
		}
		CHC = {
			set_government_rank = 2
			create_guarantee = CYI
		}
		WUU = { 
			set_government_rank = 3
			1821 = { rename_capital = "Jinling" }
		}
		HNX = { set_government_rank = 3 }
		SHU = { set_government_rank = 3 }
		WUY = { set_government_rank = 2 }
		A13 = { set_government_rank = 3 }
	}

	title = "eh_china_WUDAI.9.t"
	desc = "eh_china_WUDAI.9.d"
	picture = IMPERIAL_SEAL_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			HND = {
				every_owned_province = {
					add_core = CZH
					remove_core = HND
				}
			}
			CZH = {
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = celestial_empire
				set_government_rank = 3
				set_emperor_of_china = CZH
				add_harmonized_religion = mahayana
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "eh_china_WUDAI.9.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		CZH = {
			set_capital = 688
			add_manpower = 10
			add_sailors = 1000
			add_corruption = -10
			add_treasury = 30000
			add_years_of_income = 3
			swap_free_idea_group = yes
			inherit = HND
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Wei"
				dynasty = "Guo"
				change_adm = 4
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 4
				claim = 95
				age = 47
			}
			define_heir = {
				name = "Rong"
				dynasty = "Chai"
				change_adm = 5
				change_dip = 5
				change_mil = 5
				claim = 95
				age = 30
			}
			anhui_area = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { owned_by = CZH }
				}
				cede_province = CZH
				add_core = CZH
				remove_core = TNG
			}
			jiangsu_area = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { owned_by = CZH }
				}
				cede_province = CZH
				add_core = CZH
				remove_core = TNG
			}
			huguang_area = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { owned_by = CZH }
						NOT = { province_id = 2172 }
						NOT = { province_id = 681 }
					}
				}
				cede_province = CZH
				add_core = CZH
				remove_core = TNG
			}
			686 = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { owned_by = CZH }
					}
				}
				cede_province = CZH
				add_core = CZH
				remove_core = TNG
			}
			685 = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { owned_by = CZH }
					}
				}
				cede_province = CZH
				add_core = CZH
				remove_core = TNG
			}
			country_event = { id = eh_china_WUDAI.12 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

# Song dynasty - Event for tag
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_WUDAI.10
	title = "eh_china_WUDAI.10.t"
	desc = "eh_china_WUDAI.10.d"
	picture = IMPERIAL_SEAL_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CZH
		is_year = 960
		NOT = { is_year = 965 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			CZH = { country_event = { id = eh_china_SNG.1 days = 3 } }
			SNG = {
				688 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = SNG }
						}
					}
					cede_province = SNG
					add_core = SNG
					remove_core = CZH
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_WUDAI.10.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				CZH = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = SNG
		}
	}
}

# Jurchen
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_WUDAI.11
	title = "eh_china_WUDAI.11.t"
	desc = "eh_china_WUDAI.11.d"
	picture = IMPERIAL_SEAL_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_WUDAI.11.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		HSM = {
			set_country_flag = eh_override_name
			override_country_name = "Jurchen"
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { culture = buyeo }
				change_culture = manchu
			}
			ningguta_area = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { owned_by = HSM }
				}
				cede_province = HSM
				add_core = HSM
				remove_core = DND
			}
			hamgyeong_area = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { owned_by = HSM }
						NOT = { province_id = 732 }
					}
				}
				cede_province = HSM
				add_core = HSM
				remove_core = DND
			}
			2106 = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { owned_by = HSM }
					}
				}
				cede_province = HSM
				add_core = HSM
				remove_core = DND
			}

				limit = {
					NOT = { owned_by = NHX }
				}
				cede_province = NHX
				add_core = NHX
				remove_core = DND
			}
			furdan_area = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { owned_by = NHX }
				}
				cede_province = NHX
				add_core = NHX
				remove_core = DND
			}
		}
		NAN = {
			change_tag = CDL
			change_government = monarchy
			add_government_reform = chinese_warlord
			set_government_rank = 3
			inherit = WAA
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Siping"
				dynasty = "Duan"
				change_adm = 4
				change_dip = 3
				change_mil = 6
				claim = 95
				age = 44
			}
			define_heir = {
				dynasty = "Duan"
				male = yes
			}
			583 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = CDL }
					}
				}
				cede_province = CDL
				add_core = CDL
				remove_core = WAA
			}
			587 = {

					}

# Song dynasty
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_SNG.1
	title = "eh_china_SNG.1.t"
	desc = "eh_china_SNG.1.d"
	picture = IMPERIAL_SEAL_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			CZH = {
				every_owned_province = {
					add_core = SNG
					remove_core = CZH
				}
			}
			SNG = {
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = celestial_empire
				set_government_rank = 3
				set_emperor_of_china = SNG
				add_harmonized_religion = mahayana
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_SNG.1.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		SNG = {
			set_country_flag = song_unification
			set_capital = 688
			add_manpower = 30
			add_corruption = -10
			add_treasury = 100000
			add_years_of_income = 3
			inherit = CZH
			inherit = CYI
			swap_free_idea_group = yes
			huguang_area = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { owned_by = SNG }
				}
				cede_province = SNG
				add_core = SNG
				remove_core = JGN
			}
			hunan_area = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { owned_by = SNG }
				}
				cede_province = SNG
				add_core = SNG
				remove_core = TNG
			}
			guangxi_area = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { owned_by = SNG }
				}
				cede_province = SNG
				add_core = SNG
				remove_core = HNX
			}
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Kuangyin"
				dynasty = "Zhao"
				change_adm = 5
				change_dip = 5
				change_mil = 6
				claim = 95
				age = 33
			}
			define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 4	shock = 4	manuever = 1	siege = 2 }
			define_consort = {
				name = "Xiaoming"
				dynasty = "Wang"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				female = yes
			}
			remove_heir = { allow_new_heir = no }
		}
		TNG = { add_stability = -1 }
		SHU = { add_stability = -1 }
		HNX = { add_stability = -1 }
	}
}

# Unification of China by the Song dynasty
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_SNG.2
	title = "eh_china_SNG.2.t"
	desc = "eh_china_SNG.2.d"
	picture = REFORM_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SNG
		is_year = 975
		NOT = { is_year = 980 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			SNG = {
				inherit = SHU
				inherit = HNX
				inherit = WUY
				inherit = TNG
				inherit = HND
				china_superregion = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = SNG }
							NOT = { area = hebei_area }
							NOT = { area = gansu_area }
							NOT = { area = west_gansu_area }
							NOT = { area = taiwan_area }
							NOT = { area = yun_gui_borderland_area }
							NOT = { province_id = 662 }
							NOT = { province_id = 697 }
							NOT = { province_id = 699 }
							NOT = { province_id = 2183 }
							NOT = { province_id = 663 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = SNG
					add_core = SNG
					remove_core = TNG
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_SNG.2.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		SNG = {
			add_adm_power = 100
			add_dip_power = 100
			add_mil_power = 100
			add_stability = 1
			add_mandate = 10
			add_meritocracy_effect = yes
			add_prestige = 50
			add_years_of_income = 2
			add_army_tradition = -10
			add_army_professionalism = -0.1
			add_war_exhaustion = -10
			add_corruption = -10
			define_heir = {
				name = "Kuangyi"
				dynasty = "Zhao"
				change_adm = 5
				change_dip = 5
				change_mil = 5
				claim = 95
				age = 31
			}
			define_consort = {
				name = "Mingde"
				dynasty = "Li"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				female = yes
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = tributary_state
				subject = GYI
			}
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = DAI
				casus_belli = cb_force_tributary
			}
		}
		DAI = {
			set_country_flag = song_unification
			add_army_tradition = 10
			add_army_professionalism = 0.1
			add_years_of_income = 3
			country_event = { id = eh_asia_VTN.29 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

# Jin-Song War
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_SNG.6
	title = "eh_china_SNG.6.t"
	desc = "eh_china_SNG.6.d"
	picture = HORDE_ON_HORSEBACK_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SNG
		is_year = 1127
		NOT = { is_year = 1130 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_SNG.6.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		SNG = {
			set_country_flag = jurchen_invasion_china
			add_stability = -1
			add_mandate = -10
			add_manpower = -30
			add_army_tradition = -10
			add_army_professionalism = -0.1
		}
		CJN = {
			set_country_flag = jurchen_invasion_china
			add_stability = 1
			add_army_tradition = 10
			add_army_professionalism = 0.1
			add_manpower = 30
			north_china_region = {
				limit = { owned_by = SNG }
				change_controller = CJN
            }
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = SNG
				casus_belli = cb_horde_vs_civ
			}
			country_event = { id = eh_china_SNG.7 days = 300 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_SNG.6.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		SNG = {
			add_stability = 1
			add_prestige = -10
			add_mandate = -10
			add_treasury = -10000
		}
		CJN = {
			add_stability = 1
			add_treasury = 10000
			add_army_tradition = 10
			add_army_professionalism = 0.1
		}
	}
}

# Jingkang incident 
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_SNG.7
	title = "eh_china_SNG.7.t"
	desc = "eh_china_SNG.7.d"
	picture = HORDE_ON_HORSEBACK_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			CJN = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = nomadic_dynasty
					duration = 40000
				}
				north_china_region = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = CJN }
							NOT = { area = west_gansu_area }
							NOT = { province_id = 698 }
							NOT = { province_id = 1838 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = CJN
					add_core = CJN
					remove_core = SNG
				}
				jiangsu_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = CJN }
					}
					cede_province = CJN
					add_core = CJN
					remove_core = SNG
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_SNG.7.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		SNG = {
			clr_country_flag = jurchen_invasion_china
			set_capital = 684
			add_stability = 1
			add_mandate = 10
			white_peace = CJN
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Gou"
				dynasty = "Zhao"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 4
				change_mil = 1
				claim = 95
				age = 20
			}
			define_consort = {
				name = "Xiansheng"
				dynasty = "Wu"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				female = yes
			}
			define_heir = {
				name = "Shen"
				dynasty = "Zhao"
				change_adm = 4
				change_dip = 3
				change_mil = 3
				claim = 95
				age = 1
			}
			684 = { rename_capital = "Lin'an" }
		}
		CJN = {
			clr_country_flag = jurchen_invasion_china
			add_accepted_culture = chihan
			add_accepted_culture = hubei
			add_accepted_culture = jin
			add_accepted_culture = xibei
			add_accepted_culture = zhongyuan
			add_accepted_culture = shandong_culture
			add_war_exhaustion = -10
			688 = {
				if = {
					limit = { owned_by = CJN }
				}
				add_base_tax = -5
				add_base_production = -5
				add_base_manpower = -5
			}
		}
	}
}

# Mongol invasions of Song (1)
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_SNG.11
	title = "eh_china_SNG.11.t"
	desc = "eh_china_SNG.11.d"
	picture = MONGOL_BANNERS_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SNG
		is_year = 1260
		NOT = { is_year = 1265 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			SNG = {
				set_country_flag = mongol_invasion_china
				add_stability = -1
				add_mandate = -10
				add_manpower = -10
				add_army_tradition = -10
				add_army_professionalism = -0.1
				add_inflation = 1
				2171 = { add_building = fort_16th }
				define_advisor = {
					type = statesman
					name = "Jia Sidao"
					culture = jianghuai
					skill = 1
					discount = no
				}
				country_event = { id = eh_china_SNG.12 days = 300 }
			}
			MGE = {
				set_country_flag = mongol_invasion_china
				add_stability = 1
				add_army_tradition = 10
				add_manpower = 30
				add_sailors = 1000
				add_army_tradition = 10
				add_army_professionalism = 0.1
				add_accepted_culture = chihan
				add_accepted_culture = hubei
				add_accepted_culture = shandong_culture
				add_accepted_culture = zhongyuan
				add_accepted_culture = xibei
				add_accepted_culture = jin
				add_accepted_culture = korean
				add_accepted_culture = uyghur
				add_accepted_culture = tibetan
				add_accepted_culture = manchu
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = nomadic_dynasty
					duration = 30000
				}
				china_superregion = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = MGE }
							NOT = { owned_by = SNG }
							NOT = { area = taiwan_area }
						}
					}
					add_core = MGE
				}
				declare_war_with_cb = {
					who = SNG
					casus_belli = cb_horde_vs_civ
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_SNG.11.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				SNG = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = MGE
		}
		MGE = { country_event = { id = eh_asia_MON.52 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_SNG.11.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		MGE = { country_event = { id = eh_asia_MON.52 days = 1 } }
	}
}

		NOT = { imperial_mandate = 50 }
		YUA = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = red_turban }
		}
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}

# Unification of the Southern China by the Ming dynasty
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_MNG.2
	title = "eh_china_MNG.2.t"
	desc = "eh_china_MNG.2.d"
	picture = BATTLE_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = MNG
		is_year = 1363
		NOT = { is_year = 1368 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			MNG = {
				zhejiang_area = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { owned_by = MNG }
					}
					cede_province = MNG
					add_core = MNG
					remove_core = WUU
				}
				hunan_area = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { owned_by = MNG }
					}
					cede_province = MNG
					add_core = MNG
					remove_core = HND
				}
				shandong_area = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { owned_by = MNG }
					}
					cede_province = MNG
					add_core = MNG
					remove_core = LSO
				}
				west_shandong_area = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { owned_by = MNG }
					}
					cede_province = MNG
					add_core = MNG
					remove_core = LSO
				}
				henan_area = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { owned_by = MNG }
					}
					cede_province = MNG
					add_core = MNG
					remove_core = LSO
				}
				anhui_area = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { owned_by = MNG }
					}
					cede_province = MNG
					add_core = MNG
					remove_core = LSO
				}
				688 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = MNG }
						}
					}
					cede_province = MNG
					add_core = MNG
					remove_core = LSO
				}
				673 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = MNG }
						}
					}
					cede_province = MNG
					add_core = MNG
					remove_core = LSO
				}
				2171 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = MNG }
						}
					}
					cede_province = MNG
					add_core = MNG
					remove_core = LSO
				}
				4199 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = MNG }
						}
					}
					cede_province = MNG
					add_core = MNG
					remove_core = LSO
				}
			}
			HND = { clr_country_flag = northern_expeditions_ming }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "eh_china_MNG.2.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		MNG = {
			add_stability = 1
			add_prestige = 10
			add_corruption = -10
			add_manpower = 30
			add_sailors = 1000
			add_treasury = 10000
			add_years_of_income = 3
			add_army_tradition = 10
			add_army_professionalism = 0.1
			inherit = WUU
			inherit = HND
			inherit = LSO
			set_capital = 1821
		}
		YUA = {
			set_country_flag = northern_expeditions_ming
			remove_country_modifier = historical_mandate
			add_stability = -3
			add_mandate = -30
			add_manpower = -30
			add_prestige = -30
			add_treasury = -100000
			add_army_tradition = -30
			add_army_professionalism = -0.3
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { owned_by = YUA }
				kill_units = {
					who = YUA
					type = infantry
				}
				kill_units = {
					who = YUA
					type = cavalry
				}
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = client_kingdom
				subject = ZAO
			}
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = MNG
				casus_belli = cb_chinese_unification
			}
		}
		ZAO = {
			set_country_flag = northern_expeditions_ming
			inherit = HBN
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = eh_china_MNG.24
	title = "eh_china_MNG.24.t"
	desc = "eh_china_MNG.24.d"
	picture = CIVIL_WAR_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			MNG = {
				kill_ruler = yes
				set_capital = 1821
				add_prestige = -10
				add_mandate = -10
				add_stability = -1
				add_manpower = -10
				white_peace = CSH
			}
			CSH = {
				add_stability = -1
				add_prestige = -10
				add_war_exhaustion = 1
				create_alliance = CXI
				1816 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = CSH }
						}
					}
					cede_province = CSH
					add_core = CSH
					remove_core = MNG
				}
			}
			CXI = {
				add_stability = -1
				add_prestige = -10
				add_war_exhaustion = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_MNG.24.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		MNG = {
			china_superregion = {
				limit = { owned_by = MNG }
				kill_units = {
					who = MNG
					type = infantry
				}
				kill_units = {
					who = MNG
					type = cavalry
				}
				kill_units = {
					who = MNG
					type = artillery
				}
			}
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = CSH
				casus_belli = cb_chinese_unification
			}
		}
		QNG = { country_event = { id = eh_asia_MCH.18 days = 300 } }
	}
}

# Southern Ming dynasty
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_MNG.25
	title = "eh_china_MNG.25.t"
	desc = "eh_china_MNG.25.d"
	picture = SIEGE_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
		tag = MNG
		is_year = 1655
		NOT = { is_year = 1660 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_MNG.25.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		MNG = {
			china_superregion = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						owned_by = MNG
						NOT = { controlled_by = MNG }
					}
				}
				change_controller = MNG
				kill_units = {
					who = REB
					type = infantry
				}
				kill_units = {
					who = REB
					type = cavalry
				}
				kill_units = {
					who = REB
					type = artillery
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Notable dynasty - House of Zhu
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_MNG.26
	title = "eh_china_MNG.26.t"
	desc = "eh_china_MNG.26.d"
	picture = COURT_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
		tag = MNG
		government = monarchy
		has_regency = no
		is_year = 1368
		NOT = { is_year = 1664 }
		NOT = { dynasty = "Zhu" }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_MNG.26.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		ROOT = {
			define_ruler = {
				dynasty = "Zhu"
				male = yes
			}
			define_heir = {
				dynasty = "Zhu"
				male = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# Hongwu Emperor
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_MNG.27
	title = "eh_china_MNG.27.t"
	desc = "eh_china_MNG.27.d"
	picture = MILITARISTICALLY_TALENTED_RULER_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
		tag = MNG
		is_year = 1370
		NOT = { is_year = 1395 }
		NOT = { has_ruler = "Yuanzhang" }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_MNG.27.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		MNG = {
			change_government = monarchy
			add_government_reform = celestial_empire
			set_government_rank = 3
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Yuanzhang"
				dynasty = "Zhu"
				change_adm = 5
				change_dip = 4
				change_mil = 6
				claim = 95
				min_age = 40
				max_age = 65
			}
			define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 4	shock = 4	manuever = 3	siege = 1 }
			define_consort = {
				name = "Xiaocigao"
				dynasty = "Ma"
				change_adm = 4
				change_dip = 4
				change_mil = 4
				female = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# Qing conquest of China (1)
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_QNG.1
	title = "eh_china_QNG.1.t"
	desc = "eh_china_QNG.1.d"
	picture = MONGOL_BANNERS_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = QNG
		is_year = 1645
		NOT = { is_year = 1650 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			QNG = {
				change_primary_culture = manchu_new
				add_accepted_culture = chihan
				add_accepted_culture = hubei
				add_accepted_culture = shandong_culture
				add_accepted_culture = zhongyuan
				add_accepted_culture = xibei
				add_accepted_culture = jin
				add_stability = 1
				add_legitimacy = 10
				add_manpower = 50
				add_sailors = 1000
				inherit = CSH
				kill_leader = {
					type = "Aisin Gioro Dorgon"
				}
				define_advisor = {
					type = natural_scientist
					name = "Johann Adam Schall von Bell"
					culture = hessian
					skill = 3
					discount = yes
				}
				north_china_region = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = QNG }
							NOT = { province_id = 707 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = QNG
					add_core = QNG
					remove_core = MNG
				}
				south_china_region = {
					limit = { 
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = QNG }
							NOT = { area = guangxi_area }
							NOT = { area = taiwan_area }
							NOT = { province_id = 668 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = QNG
					add_core = QNG
					remove_core = MNG
				}
				hebei_area = {
					limit = { owned_by = QNG }
					change_culture = manchu_new
				}
				liaoning_area = {
					limit = { owned_by = QNG }
					change_culture = manchu_new
				}
				create_subject = {
					subject_type = tributary_state
					subject = KLK
				}
			}
			MNG = {
				clr_country_flag = li_zicheng_rebellion
				add_mandate = -10
				add_manpower = -10
				add_army_tradition = -10
				add_army_professionalism = -0.1
				set_capital = 667
			}
			CSH = { clr_country_flag = li_zicheng_rebellion }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_QNG.1.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				MNG = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = QNG
		}
	}
}

# Qing conquest of China (2)
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_QNG.2
	title = "eh_china_QNG.2.t"
	desc = "eh_china_QNG.2.d"
	picture = MONGOL_BANNERS_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = QNG
		is_year = 1655
		NOT = { is_year = 1660 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}

	option = {
		name = "eh_china_QNG.2.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		QNG = {
			change_government = monarchy
			add_government_reform = celestial_empire
			set_government_rank = 3
			set_emperor_of_china = QNG
			add_harmonized_religion = mahayana
			add_accepted_culture = jianghuai
			add_accepted_culture = cantonese
			add_accepted_culture = wu
			add_accepted_culture = chimin
			add_accepted_culture = sichuanese
			add_accepted_culture = xiang
			add_accepted_culture = gan
			add_stability = 1
			add_mandate = 10
			add_manpower = 50
			add_sailors = 1000
			add_war_exhaustion = -10
			inherit = CXI
			south_china_region = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { owned_by = QNG }
						NOT = { area = taiwan_area }
						NOT = { province_id = 668 }
					}
				}
				cede_province = QNG
				add_core = QNG
				remove_core = MNG
			}
			xinan_region = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { owned_by = QNG }
						NOT = { area = yun_gui_borderland_area }
					}
				}
				cede_province = QNG
				add_core = QNG
				remove_core = CXI
			}
			2170 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = QNG }
					}
				}
				cede_province = QNG
				add_core = QNG
				remove_core = CXI
			}
		}
		MNG = {
			change_government = monarchy
			add_government_reform = chinese_warlord
			set_government_rank = 3
			add_stability = -1
			add_prestige = -10
			add_manpower = -10
			set_capital = 661
		}
	}
}

# Koxinga and Wu Sangui
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_QNG.3
	title = "eh_china_QNG.3.t"
	desc = "eh_china_QNG.3.d"
	picture = CIVIL_WAR_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = QNG
		is_year = 1660
		NOT = { is_year = 1665 }
		662 = { controlled_by = QNG }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			QNG = {
				clr_country_flag = manchu_invasion_china
				define_ruler = {
					name = "Bumbutai, Borjigin"
					culture = mongol
					change_adm = 4
					change_dip = 4
					change_mil = 4
					age = 47
					female = yes
					regency = yes
				}
				define_heir = {
					name = "Hiowan yei"
					dynasty = "Aisin Gioro"
					change_adm = 6
					change_dip = 5
					change_mil = 6
					claim = 95
					age = 8
				}
				kill_leader = {
					type = "Wu Sangui"
				}
			}
			CZH = {	
				yun_gui_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = CZH }
					}
					cede_province = CZH
					add_core = CZH
				}
				yun_gui_borderland_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = CZH }
					}
					cede_province = CZH
					add_core = CZH
				}
				chuannan_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = CZH }
					}
					cede_province = CZH
					add_core = CZH
				}
				guangxi_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = CZH }
					}
					cede_province = CZH
					add_core = CZH
				}
				2174 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = CZH }
						}
					}
					cede_province = CZH
					add_core = CZH
				}
				2173 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = CZH }
						}
					}
					cede_province = CZH
					add_core = CZH
				}
			}
			A13 = {
				change_culture = chimin
				fujian_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = A13 }
					}
					cede_province = A13
					add_core = A13
				}
			}
			YUE = {
				guangzhou_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = YUE }
							NOT = { province_id = 668 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = YUE
					add_core = YUE
				}
				guangdong_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = YUE }
					}
					cede_province = YUE
					add_core = YUE
				}
				west_guangdong_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = YUE }
					}
					cede_province = YUE
					add_core = YUE
				}
			}
			ZHE = {
				taiwan_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = ZHE }
					}
					change_culture = chimin
					change_religion = confucianism
					cede_province = ZHE
					add_core = ZHE
					remove_core = NED
				}
			}
			RUS = {
				inherit = BRT
				inherit = SOL
				inherit = MYR
				manchuria_region = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = QNG }
							NOT = { province_id = 1033 }
							NOT = { province_id = 4658 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = RUS
					add_core = RUS
					remove_core = MYR
				}
				buryatia_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = RUS }
					}
					cede_province = RUS
					add_core = RUS
					remove_core = BRT
				}
			}
			MNG = { clr_country_flag = manchu_invasion_china }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_QNG.3.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		QNG = {
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = client_vassal
				subject = CZH
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = client_vassal
				subject = A13
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = client_vassal
				subject = YUE
			}
		}
		CZH = {
			change_government = monarchy
			add_government_reform = chinese_warlord
			set_government_rank = 1
			create_alliance = YUE
			create_alliance = A13
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Sangui"
				dynasty = "Wu"
				change_adm = 3
				change_dip = 3
				change_mil = 4
				claim = 95
				age = 48
			}
		}
		A13 = {
			change_government = monarchy
			add_government_reform = chinese_warlord
			set_government_rank = 1
			create_alliance = YUE
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Kexi"
				dynasty = "Shang"
				change_adm = 3
				change_dip = 4
				change_mil = 3
				claim = 95
				age = 56
			}
		}
		YUE = {
			change_government = monarchy
			add_government_reform = chinese_warlord
			set_government_rank = 1

				name = "Jingzhong"
				dynasty = "Geng"
				change_adm = 2

				age = 30
			}
		}
		ZHE = {
			change_government = monarchy

			set_government_rank = 2
			set_capital = 738
			add_stability = 1
			add_prestige = 10
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Chenggong"
				dynasty = "Zheng"

			}
			define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 5	shock = 5	manuever = 5	siege = 0 }

# The Revolt of the Three Feudatories
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_QNG.4
	title = "eh_china_QNG.4.t"
	desc = "eh_china_QNG.4.d"
	picture = CIVIL_WAR_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = QNG
		is_year = 1680
		NOT = { is_year = 1685 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			QNG = {
				set_country_flag = manchu_invasion_china
				add_manpower = 10
				add_army_tradition = 10
				add_army_professionalism = 0.1
				define_consort = {
					name = "Xiaochengren"
					dynasty = "Heseri"
					change_adm = 2
					change_dip = 2
					change_mil = 2
					female = yes
				}
				remove_heir = { allow_new_heir = no }
				country_event = { id = eh_china_QNG.5 days = 700 }
			}
			CZH = {
				set_country_flag = manchu_invasion_china
				set_government_rank = 2
				set_capital = 662
				form_coalition_against = QNG
				define_ruler = {
					name = "Sangui"
					dynasty = "Wu"
					change_adm = 3
					change_dip = 3
					change_mil = 4
					claim = 95
					age = 63
				}
				define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 2	shock = 2	manuever = 0	siege = 2	}
				define_consort = {
					name = "Yuanyuan"
					dynasty = "Chen"
					change_adm = 2
					change_dip = 2
					change_mil = 2
					female = yes
				}
				define_heir = {
					name = "Shifan"
					dynasty = "Wu"
					change_adm = 1
					change_dip = 1
					change_mil = 1
					claim = 95
					age = 25
				}
			}
			A13 = {
				set_country_flag = manchu_invasion_china
				set_government_rank = 2
				set_capital = 1829
				form_coalition_against = QNG
				define_ruler = {
					name = "Zhixin"
					dynasty = "Shang"
					change_adm = 2
					change_dip = 2
					change_mil = 2
					claim = 95
					age = 25
				}
			}
			YUE = {

# Taiping Rebellion
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_QNG.18
	title = "eh_china_QNG.18.t"
	desc = "eh_china_QNG.18.d"
	picture = ANGRY_MOB_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
		
	trigger = {
		tag = QNG
		is_year = 1855
		NOT = { is_year = 1860 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 100
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			QNG = {
				add_stability = -1
				add_prestige = -10
				add_army_tradition = -10
				add_army_professionalism = -0.1
				north_henan_area = {
					spawn_rebels = {
						type = particularist_rebels
						size = 10
						friend = TPG
					}
				}
				henan_area = {
					spawn_rebels = {
						type = particularist_rebels
						size = 10
						friend = TPG
					}
				}
			}
			TPG = {
				change_government = theocracy
				add_government_reform = theocratic_government
				set_government_rank = 3
				change_religion = reformed
				add_manpower = 30
				add_prestige = 30
				add_army_tradition = 10
				add_army_professionalism = 0.1
				add_years_of_income = 3
				set_capital = 1821
				jiangxi_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = TPG }
					}
					cede_province = TPG
					add_core = TPG
				}
				south_anhui_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = TPG }
							NOT = { province_id = 686 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = TPG
					add_core = TPG
				}
				1821 = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { owned_by = TPG }
						}
					}
					cede_province = TPG
					add_core = TPG
					infantry = TPG
					infantry = TPG
					infantry = TPG
					infantry = TPG
					infantry = TPG
					infantry = TPG
					infantry = TPG
					infantry = TPG
					cavalry = TPG
					cavalry = TPG
					cavalry = TPG
					cavalry = TPG
					artillery = TPG
					artillery = TPG
					artillery = TPG
					artillery = TPG
				}
				define_ruler = {
					name = "Xiuquan"
					dynasty = "Hong"
					change_adm = 3
					change_dip = 2
					change_mil = 4
					claim = 95
					age = 37
				}
				define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 3	shock = 3	manuever = 2	siege = 2 }
				define_consort = {
					name = "Xiying"
					dynasty = "Lai"
					change_adm = 2
					change_dip = 2
					change_mil = 2
					female = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_QNG.18.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_QNG.18.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				QNG = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = TPG
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = eh_china_QNG.19

	desc = "eh_china_QNG.19.d"
	picture = REFORM_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
		
	trigger = {
		tag = QNG
		is_year = 1860
		NOT = { is_year = 1865 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			QNG = {
				add_war_exhaustion = 2
				add_army_tradition = -10
				add_army_professionalism = -0.1
				jiangxi_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = QNG }
					}
					cede_province = QNG
					remove_core = TPG
				}
				south_anhui_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = QNG }
							NOT = { province_id = 2146 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = QNG
					remove_core = TPG
				}
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = { area = henan_area }
					spawn_rebels = {
						type = anti_tax_rebels
						size = 10
					}
				}
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = { area = west_shandong_area }
					spawn_rebels = {
						type = anti_tax_rebels
						size = 10
					}
				}
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = { area = anhui_area }
					spawn_rebels = {
						type = anti_tax_rebels
						size = 10
					}
				}
				define_ruler = {
					name = "Xingzhen, Yehe Nara"
					change_adm = 1
					change_dip = 0
					change_mil = 5
					age = 25
					claim = 95
					female = yes
					regency = yes
				}
				define_heir = {
					name = "Zaichun"
					dynasty = "Aisin Gioro"
					change_adm = 1
					change_dip = 1
					change_mil = 1
					age = 5
					claim = 95
				}
				define_general = {
					name = "Zeng Guofan"
					shock = 2
					fire = 4
					manuever = 2
					siege = 0
				}
				define_general = {
					name = "Li Hongzhang"
					shock = 3
					fire = 3
					manuever = 2
					siege = 0
				}
			}
			TPG = {
				add_stability = -1
				add_war_exhaustion = 1
				add_corruption = 10
				set_capital = 1821
				define_ruler = {
					name = "Tianguifu"
					dynasty = "Hong"
					change_adm = 0
					change_dip = 1
					change_mil = 1
					claim = 95
					age = 15
				}
				remove_heir = { allow_new_heir = no }
				south_jiangsu_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = TPG }
							NOT = { province_id = 1822 }
							NOT = { province_id = 685 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = TPG
					add_core = TPG
				}
				zhejiang_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = TPG }
							NOT = { province_id = 2149 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = TPG
					add_core = TPG
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_QNG.19.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		TPG = {
			set_country_flag = taiping_rebellion
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = QNG
				casus_belli = cb_chinese_unification
			}
		}
		QNG = { 
			set_country_flag = taiping_rebellion
			country_event = { id = eh_china_QNG.20 days = 300 }
		}
	}
}

				discount = yes
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				add_institution_embracement = {
					which = imperialism
					value = 50
				}
				add_institution_embracement = {
					which = industrialization
					value = 20
				}
				add_institution_embracement = {
					which = nationalism_institution
					value = 40
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Boxer Protocol
country_event = {

					is_subject_of = QNG

# Wuchang Uprising
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_QNG.30
	title = "eh_china_QNG.30.t"
	desc = "eh_china_QNG.30.d"
	picture = REVOLUTION_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = QNG
		is_year = 1911
		NOT = { is_year = 1912 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			ROC = {
				change_government = republic
				add_government_reform = multi_party_system
				set_government_rank = 3
				set_capital = 682
				add_adm_power = 100
				add_dip_power = 100
				add_mil_power = 100
				add_stability = 1
				add_manpower = 50
				add_sailors = 1000
				add_prestige = 30
				add_years_of_income = 3
				add_army_tradition = 10
				add_army_professionalism = 0.1
				change_religion = secularism
				huguang_area = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { owned_by = ROC }
					}
					cede_province = ROC
					add_core = ROC
					remove_core = QNG
				}
			}
			QNG = {
				remove_country_modifier = nomadic_dynasty
				remove_accepted_culture = chihan
				remove_accepted_culture = hubei
				remove_accepted_culture = shandong_culture
				remove_accepted_culture = zhongyuan
				remove_accepted_culture = jianghuai
				remove_accepted_culture = xibei
				remove_accepted_culture = cantonese
				remove_accepted_culture = wu
				remove_accepted_culture = sichuanese
				remove_accepted_culture = xiang
				remove_accepted_culture = gan
				remove_accepted_culture = jin
				country_event = { id = eh_china_QNG.31 days = 100 } 
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_QNG.30.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		ROC = {
			change_primary_culture = jianghuai
			add_accepted_culture = chihan
			add_accepted_culture = hubei
			add_accepted_culture = shandong_culture
			add_accepted_culture = zhongyuan
			add_accepted_culture = xibei
			add_accepted_culture = cantonese
			add_accepted_culture = wu
			add_accepted_culture = chimin
			add_accepted_culture = sichuanese
			add_accepted_culture = xiang
			add_accepted_culture = gan
			add_accepted_culture = jin
			add_treasury = 100000
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Sun Yat-sen"
				change_adm = 4
				change_dip = 5
				change_mil = 1
				age = 42
			}
		}
		QNG = { 
			add_treasury = -100000
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Zaifeng, Aisin Gioro"
				change_adm = 1
				change_dip = 1
				change_mil = 1
				claim = 95
				regency = yes
			}
			define_heir = {
				name = "Puyi"
				dynasty = "Aisin Gioro"
				change_adm = 3
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 1
				age = 3
				claim = 95
			}
		}
	}
}

# Xinhai Revolution
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_QNG.31
	title = "eh_china_QNG.31.t"
	desc = "eh_china_QNG.31.d"
	picture = REVOLUTION_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			ROC = {
				set_country_flag = xinhai_revolution
				set_capital = 1821
				add_government_reform = democracy_reform
				add_manpower = 50
				add_sailors = 1000
				add_army_tradition = 10
				add_army_professionalism = 0.1
				add_republican_tradition = 10
				add_years_of_income = 3
				north_china_region = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { area = gansu_area }
							NOT = { area = west_gansu_area }
							NOT = { area = hebei_area }
							NOT = { area = south_hebei_area }
							NOT = { province_id = 2019 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = ROC
					add_core = ROC
					remove_core = QNG
				}
				south_china_region = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = ROC }
							NOT = { area = taiwan_area }
							NOT = { province_id = 668 }
							NOT = { province_id = 3005 }
						}
					}
					infantry = ROC
					infantry = ROC
					cede_province = ROC
					add_core = ROC
					remove_core = QNG
				}
				xinan_region = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = ROC }
					}
					cavalry = ROC
					artillery = ROC
					cede_province = ROC
					add_core = ROC
					remove_core = QNG
				}
				country_event = { id = eh_china_CHN.1 days = 300 }
			}
			QNG = {
				remove_country_modifier = historical_mandate
				set_country_flag = xinhai_revolution
				add_stability = -1
				add_prestige = -10
				add_mandate = -10
				add_army_tradition = -10
				add_army_professionalism = -0.1
				add_years_of_income = -2
				china_superregion = {
					limit = { owned_by = QNG }
					kill_units = {
						who = QNG
						type = infantry
					}
					kill_units = {
						who = QNG
						type = cavalry
					}
					kill_units = {
						who = QNG
						type = artillery
					}
				}
				declare_war_with_cb = {
					who = ROC
					casus_belli = cb_imperial
				}
				country_event = { id = eh_asia_MON.36 days = 100 }
			}
			TIB = {
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = tibetan_dual_government_reform
				set_government_rank = 3
				change_religion = vajrayana
				define_ruler = {
					name = "Thubten Gyatso"
					change_adm = 3
					change_dip = 3
					change_mil = 2
					age = 1
					claim = 95
				}
				tibet_region = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = TIB }
							NOT = { area = bhutan_area }
							NOT = { area = amdo_area }
							NOT = { area = kham_area }
							NOT = { province_id = 4522 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = TIB
					add_core = TIB
					remove_core = QNG
				}
				2131 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = TIB }
						}
					}
					cede_province = TIB
					add_core = TIB
					remove_core = QNG
				}
				2132 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = TIB }
						}
					}
					cede_province = TIB
					add_core = TIB
					remove_core = QNG
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_QNG.31.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				QNG = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = ROC
		}
	}
}

				NOT = { has_country_flag = taiping_rebellion }

		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}

	}

				name = historical_mandate

			}
		}
	}

	major = yes

		name = "eh_china_CHN.1.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		ROC = {
			clr_country_flag = xinhai_revolution
			change_primary_culture = chihan
			change_technology_group = asian
			add_republican_tradition = 10
			set_capital = 1816
			dismantle_empire_of_china = yes
			inherit = QNG
			hebei_area = { change_culture = chihan }
			every_owned_province = {
				add_institution_embracement = {
					which = industrialization
					value = 10
				}
				add_institution_embracement = {
					which = nationalism_institution
					value = 40
				}
				add_institution_embracement = {
					which = electrification
					value = 30
				}
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = autonomous_state
				subject = TIB
			}
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Yuan Shikai"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 6
				age = 53
			}
		}
		QNG = { clr_country_flag = xinhai_revolution }
	}
}

country_event = {

			FRM = {
				set_country_flag = northern_expedition_china
				add_adm_power = 100
				add_dip_power = 100
				add_mil_power = 100
				add_stability = 3
				add_manpower = 50
				add_sailors = 1000
				add_republican_tradition = 10
				add_army_tradition = 10
				add_army_professionalism = 0.1
				add_prestige = 30
				add_treasury = 50000
				add_years_of_income = 3
				add_war_exhaustion = -10

					name = major_power
					duration = 10000
				}

						NOT = { owned_by = FRM }

					remove_core = ROC
				}

						owned_by = CFT

							NOT = { owned_by = FRM }

					remove_core = ROC
				}

						NOT = { owned_by = CFT }

					add_core = CFT
					remove_core = CZL
				}
				shandong_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = CFT }
					}
					cede_province = CFT
					add_core = CFT
					remove_core = CZL
				}
				west_shandong_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = CFT }
					}
					cede_province = CFT
					add_core = CFT
					remove_core = CZL
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_ROC.2.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

# Mukden Incident
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_ROC.5
	title = "eh_china_ROC.5.t"
	desc = "eh_china_ROC.5.d"
	picture = WW_ALLIES_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = {
				manchuria_region = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = JAP }
							NOT = { area = east_heilongjiang_area }
							NOT = { area = central_ilin_hala_area }
							NOT = { area = ilan_hala_area }
							NOT = { area = central_jilin_area }
							NOT = { area = furdan_area }
						}
					}
					cede_province = JAP
					add_core = JAP
					remove_core = CFT
				}
				chahar_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = JAP }
							NOT = { province_id = 2115 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = JAP
					add_core = JAP
					remove_core = CFT
				}
				cicigar_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = JAP }

						NOT = { owned_by = JAP }

					remove_core = CFT

				703 = {

# Chinese Soviet Republic
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_PRC.1
	title = "eh_china_PRC.1.t"
	desc = "eh_china_PRC.1.d"
	picture = COMMUNISM_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = FRM
		is_year = 1930
		NOT = { is_year = 1935 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	
	immediate = {
		CHN = {
			670 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = CHN }
					}
				}
				cede_province = CHN
				add_core = CHN
			}
			2151 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = CHN }
					}
				}
				cede_province = CHN
				add_core = CHN
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_PRC.1.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		CHN = {
			set_country_flag = eh_communist
			set_country_flag = eh_override_name
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = communist_government
			set_government_rank = 2
			change_technology_group = asian
			add_historical_friend = SOV
			add_historical_rival = FRM
			change_religion = secularism
			change_country_color = { color = { 194  53  60 } }
			override_country_name = "Communist China"
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Bo Gu"
				change_adm = 1
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				age = 24
			}
		}
		FRM = {
			add_historical_rival = CHN
			country_event = { id = eh_china_PRC.2 days = 30 }
		}
	}
}
