# Second Chinese Civil War
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_ROC.11
	title = "eh_china_ROC.11.t"
	desc = "eh_china_ROC.11.d"
	picture = WW_ALLIES_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_ROC.11.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		FRM = {
			set_country_flag = chinese_civil_war
			add_stability = -1
			add_prestige = -10
			add_manpower = -50
			add_sailors = -3000
			add_army_tradition = -10
			add_army_professionalism = -0.1
			add_historical_rival = CHN
			remove_historical_friend = CHN
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
				change_adm = 3
				change_dip = 3
				change_mil = 5
				age = 50
			}
			define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 3	shock = 3	manuever = 3	siege = 0 }
			south_china_region = {
				limit = { owned_by = FRM }
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = communist_rebels
					size = 1				
				}
			}
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = CHN
				casus_belli = cb_chinese_unification
			}
			country_event = { id = eh_china_ROC.12 days = 700 }
		}
		CHN = {
			set_country_flag = chinese_civil_war
			add_stability = 1
			add_prestige = 10
			add_manpower = 100
			add_sailors = 3000
			add_army_tradition = 10
			add_army_professionalism = 0.1
			add_historical_rival = FRM
			remove_historical_friend = FRM
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Mao Zedong"
				change_adm = 1
				change_dip = 4
				change_mil = 6
				age = 54
			}
			define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 3	shock = 3	manuever = 4	siege = 0 }
			country_event = { id = eh_asia_CHN.27 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

	desc = "eh_china_PRC.8.d"
	picture = FAMINE_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CHN
		is_year = 1958
		NOT = { is_year = 1962 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_PRC.8.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		CHN = { 
			add_army_tradition = -10
			add_army_professionalism = -0.1
			add_stability = -1
			add_prestige = -10
			add_corruption = 10
			add_inflation = 1
			add_manpower = -100
			add_adm_power = -100
			add_dip_power = -100
			add_mil_power = -100
			add_years_of_income = -1
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Mao Zedong"
				change_adm = 1
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				age = 71
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { province_id = 667 }
						NOT = { province_id = 695 }
						NOT = { province_id = 1816 }
						NOT = { province_id = 1821 }
						NOT = { province_id = 1822 }
					}
				}
				add_devastation = 30
				add_base_tax = -5
				add_base_production = -5
				add_base_manpower = -1
			}
		}
		HKG = {
			3005 = {
				add_prosperity = 20
				add_base_tax = 20
				add_base_production = 20
				add_base_manpower = 20
				change_trade_goods = electronics
			}
		}

# Rise of the Deng Xiaoping
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_PRC.11
	title = "eh_china_PRC.11.t"
	desc = "eh_china_PRC.11.d"
	picture = REFORM_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CHN
		is_year = 1978
		NOT = { is_year = 1980 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_PRC.11.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		CHN = {
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = communist_government
			add_adm_power = 100
			add_dip_power = 100
			add_mil_power = 100
			add_prestige = 10
			add_stability = 3
			add_inflation = -3
			add_years_of_income = 1
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Deng Xiaoping"
				change_adm = 5
				change_dip = 5
				change_mil = 5
				age = 74
			}
			china_superregion = {
				limit = { owned_by = CHN }
				add_prosperity = 3
				add_base_tax = 3
				add_base_production = 3
				add_base_manpower = 3
				add_institution_embracement = {
					which = globalization
					value = 50
				}
			}
			manchuria_region = {
				limit = { owned_by = CHN }
				add_prosperity = 3
				add_base_tax = 1
				add_base_production = 1
				add_base_manpower = 1
			}
		}
		FRM = {
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = democracy_reform
			set_government_rank = 2
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Chiang Ching-kuo"
				change_adm = 4
				change_dip = 3
				change_mil = 3
				age = 68
			}
		}
	}
}

# Hong Kong protests
country_event = {
	id = eh_china_PRC.21
	title = "eh_china_PRC.21.t"
	desc = "eh_china_PRC.21.d"
	picture = STREET_SPEECH_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CHN
		is_year = 2010
		NOT = { is_year = 2020 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 700
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_PRC.21.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		CHN = {
			add_prestige = -10
			3005 = { add_unrest = 10 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_china_PRC.21.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		CHN = { add_prestige = 10 }
		HKG = {
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = democracy_reform
			set_government_rank = 2
			add_stability = 1
			add_prestige = 10
			add_adm_power = 100
			add_dip_power = 100
			add_mil_power = 100
			add_years_of_income = 5
			3005 = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { owned_by = HKG }
					}
				}
				cede_province = HKG
				add_core = HKG
				remove_core = CHN
			}
		}
	}
}

# Spread of Buddhism to China
country_event = {
	id = eh_asia_CHN.1
	title = "eh_asia_CHN.1.t"
	desc = "eh_asia_CHN.1.d"
	picture = BUDDHA_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			culture_group = east_asian
			is_emperor_of_china = yes
			AND = {
				religion = confucianism
				NOT = { religion = mahayana }
				NOT = { religion = vajrayana }
			}
		}
		is_year = 100
		NOT = { is_year = 960 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1000
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_asia_CHN.1.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		ROOT = {
			change_religion = confucianism
			add_harmonized_religion = mahayana
			add_harmonized_religion = vajrayana
			add_prestige = 10
		}
	}
}
